## Project Structure

```sh
└── aida-web/
    ├── eslint.config.js
    ├── index.html
    ├── node_modules
    │   ├── .bin
    │   ├── .package-lock.json
    │   ├── @alloc
    │   ├── @isaacs
    │   ├── @jridgewell
    │   ├── @nodelib
    │   ├── @pkgjs
    │   ├── @types
    │   ├── ansi-regex
    │   ├── ansi-styles
    │   ├── any-promise
    │   ├── anymatch
    │   ├── arg
    │   ├── balanced-match
    │   ├── binary-extensions
    │   ├── brace-expansion
    │   ├── braces
    │   ├── camelcase-css
    │   ├── chokidar
    │   ├── classnames
    │   ├── color-convert
    │   ├── color-name
    │   ├── commander
    │   ├── cookie
    │   ├── cross-spawn
    │   ├── cssesc
    │   ├── didyoumean
    │   ├── dlv
    │   ├── eastasianwidth
    │   ├── emoji-regex
    │   ├── enquire.js
    │   ├── fast-glob
    │   ├── fastq
    │   ├── fill-range
    │   ├── foreground-child
    │   ├── function-bind
    │   ├── glob
    │   ├── glob-parent
    │   ├── hasown
    │   ├── is-binary-path
    │   ├── is-core-module
    │   ├── is-extglob
    │   ├── is-fullwidth-code-point
    │   ├── is-glob
    │   ├── is-number
    │   ├── isexe
    │   ├── jackspeak
    │   ├── jiti
    │   ├── json2mq
    │   ├── lilconfig
    │   ├── lines-and-columns
    │   ├── lodash.debounce
    │   ├── lru-cache
    │   ├── merge2
    │   ├── micromatch
    │   ├── minimatch
    │   ├── minipass
    │   ├── mz
    │   ├── nanoid
    │   ├── normalize-path
    │   ├── object-assign
    │   ├── object-hash
    │   ├── package-json-from-dist
    │   ├── path-key
    │   ├── path-parse
    │   ├── path-scurry
    │   ├── picocolors
    │   ├── picomatch
    │   ├── pify
    │   ├── pirates
    │   ├── postcss
    │   ├── postcss-import
    │   ├── postcss-js
    │   ├── postcss-load-config
    │   ├── postcss-nested
    │   ├── postcss-selector-parser
    │   ├── postcss-value-parser
    │   ├── queue-microtask
    │   ├── react
    │   ├── react-dom
    │   ├── react-router
    │   ├── react-router-dom
    │   ├── react-slick
    │   ├── read-cache
    │   ├── readdirp
    │   ├── resize-observer-polyfill
    │   ├── resolve
    │   ├── reusify
    │   ├── run-parallel
    │   ├── scheduler
    │   ├── set-cookie-parser
    │   ├── shebang-command
    │   ├── shebang-regex
    │   ├── signal-exit
    │   ├── slick-carousel
    │   ├── source-map-js
    │   ├── string-convert
    │   ├── string-width
    │   ├── string-width-cjs
    │   ├── strip-ansi
    │   ├── strip-ansi-cjs
    │   ├── sucrase
    │   ├── supports-preserve-symlinks-flag
    │   ├── swiper
    │   ├── tailwindcss
    │   ├── thenify
    │   ├── thenify-all
    │   ├── to-regex-range
    │   ├── ts-interface-checker
    │   ├── turbo-stream
    │   ├── util-deprecate
    │   ├── which
    │   ├── wrap-ansi
    │   ├── wrap-ansi-cjs
    │   └── yaml
    ├── package-lock.json
    ├── package.json
    ├── public
    │   └── vite.svg
    ├── src
    │   ├── App.css
    │   ├── App.jsx
    │   ├── Canvas
    │   ├── components
    │   ├── Home.jsx
    │   ├── index.css
    │   └── main.jsx
    ├── tailwind.config.js
    └── vite.config.js
```

## Getting Started

### Prerequisites

This project requires the following dependencies:

- **Programming Language:** JavaScript
- **Package Manager:** Npm, Bower

### Installation

Build aida-web from the source and intsall dependencies:

1. **Clone the repository:**

    ```sh
    ❯ git clone ../aida-web
    ```

2. **Navigate to the project directory:**

    ```sh
    ❯ cd aida-web
    ```

3. **Install the dependencies:**

<!-- SHIELDS BADGE CURRENTLY DISABLED -->
	<!-- [![npm][npm-shield]][npm-link] -->
	<!-- REFERENCE LINKS -->
	<!-- [npm-shield]: https://img.shields.io/badge/npm-CB3837.svg?style={badge_style}&logo=npm&logoColor=white -->
	<!-- [npm-link]: https://www.npmjs.com/ -->

	**Using [npm](https://www.npmjs.com/):**

	```sh
	❯ npm install
	```
<!-- SHIELDS BADGE CURRENTLY DISABLED -->
	<!-- [![bower][bower-shield]][bower-link] -->
	<!-- REFERENCE LINKS -->
	<!-- [bower-shield]: None -->
	<!-- [bower-link]: None -->

	**Using [bower](None):**

	```sh
	❯ echo 'INSERT-INSTALL-COMMAND-HERE'
	```

### Usage

Run the project with:

**Using [npm](https://www.npmjs.com/):**
```sh
npm start
```
**Using [bower](None):**
```sh
echo 'INSERT-RUN-COMMAND-HERE'
```

### Testing

Aida-web uses the {__test_framework__} test framework. Run the test suite with:

**Using [npm](https://www.npmjs.com/):**
```sh
npm test
```
**Using [bower](None):**
```sh
echo 'INSERT-TEST-COMMAND-HERE'
```

## Contributing

- **💬 [Join the Discussions](https://LOCAL//aida-web/discussions)**: Share your insights, provide feedback, or ask questions.
- **🐛 [Report Issues](https://LOCAL//aida-web/issues)**: Submit bugs found or log feature requests for the `aida-web` project.
- **💡 [Submit Pull Requests](https://LOCAL//aida-web/blob/main/CONTRIBUTING.md)**: Review open PRs, and submit your own PRs.

<details closed>
<summary>Contributing Guidelines</summary>

1. **Fork the Repository**: Start by forking the project repository to your LOCAL account.
2. **Clone Locally**: Clone the forked repository to your local machine using a git client.
   ```sh
   git clone aida-web
   ```
3. **Create a New Branch**: Always work on a new branch, giving it a descriptive name.
   ```sh
   git checkout -b new-feature-x
   ```
4. **Make Your Changes**: Develop and test your changes locally.
5. **Commit Your Changes**: Commit with a clear message describing your updates.
   ```sh
   git commit -m 'Implemented new feature x.'
   ```
6. **Push to LOCAL**: Push the changes to your forked repository.
   ```sh
   git push origin new-feature-x
   ```
7. **Submit a Pull Request**: Create a PR against the original project repository. Clearly describe the changes and their motivations.
8. **Review**: Once your PR is reviewed and approved, it will be merged into the main branch. Congratulations on your contribution!
</details>

<details closed>
<summary>Contributor Graph</summary>
<br>
<p align="left">
   <a href="https://LOCAL{//aida-web/}graphs/contributors">
      <img src="https://contrib.rocks/image?repo=/aida-web">
   </a>
</p>
</details>
